							<div class="seo-description-copy-short">
								Did you know that a car seat is the only baby gear item you're legally required to buy? 
								
									<a class="seemore">see more</a>
								
							</div>
							<div class="seo-description-copy-long hide">
								Did you know that a car seat is the only baby gear item you're legally required to buy? Even if you don't have a car, most hospitals won't let you take your newborn baby home until you have them securely fastened in a car seat. That's why it's an absolute <a href="http://www.giggle.com/Top-10-Must-Haves/top-10-must-haves,default,pg.html">registry must-have</a>. There are four basic types of car seats you need to know about, and you can read up on all of them in our <a href="http://www.giggle.com/Car-Seats/gear-guides-car-seats,default,pg.html">Car Seat Guide</a>. The difference between them has to do with the size your child. Up first: Infant car seats. Designed to fit babies up to 6-9 months, they're made to be portable, so you can switch your sleeping baby in and out of the car easily. Toddler seats hold children from around 6 months of age until about 4 years or 40 lbs,. and remain rear-facing in your car until your baby is 1-year-old. Once your little one has outgrown a toddler seat, transition them to a booster seat. It's basically a mini version of a regular car seat with added safety features and a weight capacity of up to 100 lbs. Your other option? Save money and buy a convertible car seat, which can either transition from infant seat to toddler seat or toddler seat to booster seat! Browse our picks now, and then add it to your registry in a snap, with our <a href="http://www.giggle.com/on/demandware.store/Sites-giggle-Site/default/GiftRegistry-ShowChecklist">Quick-Click Registry Checklist</a>. <a class="seeless">see less</a>
							</div>

It's a high-performance automotive-grade fabric that's super-durable and very easy to care for.<br /><br />Clek's Foonf in Phantom does not include side-bolster magnets, as Clek has phased-out this feature from their Foonf product.</div><div class="BVQAContentData BVAnswerData"> <div class="BVQAElapsedTime">2 weeks, 5 days ago</div>

Answers </h2>

<div class="BVQABadges BVQAAnswerBadges"> <div
class="BVQABadge BVQAAnswerBadge BVQAStaffBadge"
title="Staff Answer">
<img class="BVQABadgeIcon BVQAAnswerBadgeIcon BVQAStaffIcon" src="http://giggle.ugc.bazaarvoice.com/answers/6890/static/staff-icon.gif" alt="Staff Answer" />

<div class="BVQAAnswerRight">
<div class="BVQAContentText BVQAAnswerText"><div class="BVQAContentLabel BVQAAnswerLabel">A: </div>Like all car seats, Cybex Aton's seat cover is designed to be very taut and to exactly fit inside the Infant Carrier. If you want to wash the cover before using your car seat, you'll want to pay close attention before and during the removal of the cover to help remember how to put it back on.<br /><br />The seat cover, shoulder pads, buckle pad, and the infant insert can be machine washed cold, gentle cycle, with mild detergent...no bleach, please! Line-dry, rather than machine dry, all of these parts, and ironing isn't recommended.<br /><br />For a complete list of Care and Cleaning Instructions, consult your Cybex Aton Owner's Manual.</div><div class="BVQAContentData BVAnswerData"> <div class="BVQAElapsedTime">1 month, 2 weeks ago</div>

<div class="BVQAContentText BVQAAnswerText"><div class="BVQAContentLabel BVQAAnswerLabel">A: </div>All of the car seats in giggle's assortment meet (and most exceed!) safety standards set by the NHTSA (National Highway Traffic Safety Administration). And, since safety is the most important consideration when choosing — and using — a car seat, here's what you should know:<br /><br />• The NHTSA (National Highway Traffic Safety Administration) sets and maintains national standards for all car seats sold in the United States. Every car seat sold in the U.S. must meet/exceed NHTSA standards.<br />• Each state sets their own &quot;best practice&quot; laws for the use of car seats – like how much a child must weigh, or how old or tall they are to position car seats a certain way, or use them at all.<br />• Proper use and installation instructions from the manufacturer come will all car seats.<br /><br />Chicco's KeyFit and UppaBaby's Mesa are both awesome seats and each has a &quot;reason for being&quot; in giggle's assortment. Here's some information to help you with your decision:<br /><br />• Chicco KeyFit: A top performer in Consumer Reports for “Ease of Use” KeyFit boasts very EASY installation for parents with its centralized LATCH system.<br />• UppaBaby Mesa: giggle’s EASY 10-second installation story for our UppaBaby customers, Mesa completes a true UppaBaby traditional Travel System solution.</div><div class="BVQAAnswerProductReferencesDiv"><div class="BVDI BVDI_PL"><div class="BVDISeparator BVDI_PLSeparatorTop">&nbsp;</div><div class="BVDIHeader BVDI_PLHeader"><div class="BVDITitle BVDI_PLTitle">Products from my answer</div></div><div class="BVDIBody BVDI_PLBody"><div class="BVDI_PLHelperText"></div>

<div class="BVQAContentText BVQAAnswerText"><div class="BVQAContentLabel BVQAAnswerLabel">A: </div>As a rule, convertible car seats, including MaxiCosi's Pria 70, don't have the option of adapting to a stroller for quick in-and-out-of-the-car convenience.<br /><br />The exception to that rule is Orbit's Toddler Car Seat, a convertible car seat for a child 15+ lbs. that adapts to Orbit's Baby Stroller Base G2.<br /><br />If car-seat-to-stroller compatibility for a newborn is what you're looking for, make sure to view giggle's Infant Car Seat assortment. All will adapt to strollers with the addition of the matching infant car seat adapter accessory (i.e. for a MaxiCosi Mico choose your stroller brand's MaxiCosi Mico Car Seat Adapter).<br /><br />Still have questions? giggle's Customer Service Team is ready to help -- give us a call at 1-800-495-8577, or email us at customerservice@giggle.com.</div><div class="BVQAAnswerProductReferencesDiv"><div class="BVDI BVDI_PL"><div class="BVDISeparator BVDI_PLSeparatorTop">&nbsp;</div><div class="BVDIHeader BVDI_PLHeader"><div class="BVDITitle BVDI_PLTitle">Products from my answer</div></div><div class="BVDIBody BVDI_PLBody"><div class="BVDI_PLHelperText"></div>

<script type="text/javascript">
	jQuery.ajax({
		  url: '/on/demandware.store/Sites-giggle-Site/default/ltkClickTracking-Start' + '?' + document.location.search,
		  context: document,
		  success: function(trkt){
			  var start = trkt.indexOf('[');
			  var end = trkt.indexOf(']');
			  var token = trkt.substring(start+1, end); 
			  setCookie("_trkt", token, 365, null, '/'); 
			  }
		});
	
	function setCookie(c_name,value,exdays, domain, path, secure)
	{
		if (value != '' && value != undefined)
		{
	        var exd = new Date();
	        exd.setDate(exd.getDate() + exdays);
	        document.cookie =
	        	c_name + "=" + encodeURIComponent(value) +
		        ((exdays == null) ? "" : "; expires=" + exd.toGMTString()) +
		        ((domain == null && domain != "") ? "" : "; domain=" + domain) +
		        ((path == null) ? "" : "; path=" + path) +
		        ((secure) ? "; secure" : "");			
		}
	}	
</script> 





	<script type="text/javascript">
	var _ltkwmt = 'enter e-mail,* Email Address &#40;required&#41;';
	function isWatermark(wmt) {
	    if(!_ltkwmt || _ltkwmt.length == 0) {
	        return false;
	    }
	    if(_ltkwmt.indexOf(wmt) >= 0) { 
	        return true; 
	    }
	    else { return false; }
	}
		
	function ltkCaptureEmail(id) {
	    try {
	        var _stsi1 = setInterval(function () {
	            if (!window.jQuery) { return; }
	            clearInterval(_stsi1);
	            if (typeof id == "undefined" || id == "") { return; }
	            var _sl = jQuery("[id='" + id + "']");
	            if (_sl.length == 0) { _sl = jQuery("input[name='" + id + "']"); }
	            if (_sl.length) {
	                _sl.change(function () { 
			                if (jQuery(_sl).val().length > 0 && !isWatermark(jQuery(_sl).val()))
			                {
			                	jQuery.ajax({
			              		  url: '/on/demandware.store/Sites-giggle-Site/default/ltkEmailCapture-Start' + '?email=' + jQuery(this).val(),
			              		  context: document,
			              		  success: function(success){ return; }
			              		});
			                }
						}
	                );
	                if (jQuery(_sl).val().length > 0 && !isWatermark(jQuery(_sl).val())) { _ltk.SCA.Update("email", jQuery(_sl).val()); }
	            }
	        }, 100);
	    }
	    catch (ex) {
	        _ltk.Exception.Submit(ex, 'CaptureEmail');
	    }
	}
	
		ltkCaptureEmail("dwfrm_profile_customer_email");
	
		ltkCaptureEmail("dwfrm_login_username");
	
		ltkCaptureEmail("dwfrm_billing_billingAddress_email_emailAddress");
